<div id="review_2197078346" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2197078346" />
    <a title="The Captain" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54489623-the-captain"><img alt="The Captain" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459976325p2/54489623.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2197078346?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="The Captain" class="user" itemprop="url" name="The Captain" href="/user/show/54489623-the-captain">The Captain</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54489623-the-captain?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2197078346" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16755612004956016544">Ahoy there me mateys! This be me read for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/19408177-july-theme-reviews' rel='nofollow noopener'>the July BookBum Club Challenge</a> where the theme be “that is so last year – a book ye meant to read in 2017.” Well Dean Koontz is one of me favourite authors and was featured in Broadside No. 9 but I hadn’t read a book by him since 2011! This book marks me 60th Dean Koontz book. Arrrr! It was about time I got to it because books two and three are already out. Plus book four is coming soon. I have been wanting to read this ever since I read crew member, <a href='https://cadburypom.wordpress.com/2017/06/21/the-silent-corner-jane-hawk-1-by-dean-koontz-4-5-stars/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ki</a></span>
  <span id="freeText16755612004956016544" style="display:none">Ahoy there me mateys! This be me read for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/topic/show/19408177-july-theme-reviews" rel="nofollow noopener">the July BookBum Club Challenge</a> where the theme be “that is so last year – a book ye meant to read in 2017.” Well Dean Koontz is one of me favourite authors and was featured in Broadside No. 9 but I hadn’t read a book by him since 2011! This book marks me 60th Dean Koontz book. Arrrr! It was about time I got to it because books two and three are already out. Plus book four is coming soon. I have been wanting to read this ever since I read crew member, <a href="https://cadburypom.wordpress.com/2017/06/21/the-silent-corner-jane-hawk-1-by-dean-koontz-4-5-stars/" rel="nofollow noopener">Kim @ byhookorbybook’s review back in 2017</a>! Now be the time.<br /><br />The very basic premise is that the suicide rate in the United States has been higher than average and seems to be steadily increasing. One of the victims is Nick Hawk, a husband, father, and highly decorated marine. Everyone believes that he committed suicide except for his wife, Jane. Jane Hawk, FBI agent, knows that her husband would never have killed himself. His odd “suicide” note is proof of that. So she starts digging determined to uncover the truth behind Nick’s death. But the answers are even stranger then she thought. Can she take the evil doers down before they get to her first?<br /><br />Of course it is so much more complicated and cooler than that. What I love about Dean Koontz is that he can write a fantastic thriller with sci-fi bits. And the sci-fi is plausible in our not too distant future. I can’t go into more than that because it is part of the fun of readin’ this one. The science of it is both scary and fascinating. This book also deals with the silent corner – i.e. people who try to stay completely off the grid. In the modern era of Big Brother, it does seem like this will be impossible in the future. Watching Jane try to stay off the grid while needing the internet for research is interesting. And darn near impossible.<br /><br />This book had a fantastically quick pace and I read it in one sitting. I was completely rooting for Jane. She is smart, clever, and fierce. The bad guys were a bit one dimensional and the final showdown was silly but that didn’t lessen me enjoyment. I certainly got what I wanted out of this book and will not be waiting another seven years to pick up another Dean Koontz book. I need more Jane Hawk!<br /><br />Much thanks to the BookBum Club for giving me the incentive to read this “so last year” novel.<br /><br />Check out me other reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://thecaptainsquartersblog.wordpress.com/">https://thecaptainsquartersblog.wordp...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="16755612004956016544" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1950239016" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1950239016" />

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1379514-magdalena-aka-a-bookaholic-swede?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1950239016" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13381048719061886745">I read Lightning by Dean Koontz many, many years ago and since then I have loved Dean Koontz's books. I haven't read that many Koontz books in recent years, but I have slowly started to read through the books I have missed. I was really thrilled to get the chase to read The Silent Corner, the first book in a new thriller series.<br/><br/>The book starts off strong with the book's heroine Jane Hawk trying to find a reason for why her husband and several other people have committed suicide, despite never sh</span>
  <span id="freeText13381048719061886745" style="display:none">I read Lightning by Dean Koontz many, many years ago and since then I have loved Dean Koontz's books. I haven't read that many Koontz books in recent years, but I have slowly started to read through the books I have missed. I was really thrilled to get the chase to read The Silent Corner, the first book in a new thriller series.<br /><br />The book starts off strong with the book's heroine Jane Hawk trying to find a reason for why her husband and several other people have committed suicide, despite never showing any sign of being depressed. What she learns will make her run for her life as she also tries to find a way to stop people who will stop at nothing to silence her.<br /><br />I found the book to be both intriguing and thrilling to read. I love that the books start off strong, no slow starts to ease into the story. Instead, BAM and away. Since this is the first book in a series will the book of course not answer all the questions, but it's a satisfying ending and I felt that I really wanted the next book after I finished The Silent Corner.<br /><br />This is a perfect book for thriller fans!<br /><br /><i>Thanks to <a href="http://bokfabriken.se/" rel="nofollow noopener">Bokfabriken</a> for the review copy!</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13381048719061886745" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2068162831" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2068162831" />
    <a title="Annie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69270382-annie"><img alt="Annie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1522188916p2/69270382.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2068162831?book_show_action=true">Aug 06, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie" href="/user/show/69270382-annie">Annie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover " href="/book/show/35563270-the-silent-corner">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69270382-annie?shelf=2017-reads">2017-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2068162831" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6327698030875170074">Koontz is one of my favourite authors, but I've not read any of his books for years. Over the years, I have seen the 'series' of books become more and more popular with authors. Having read The Silent Corner, I now have to wait months for the next instalment of the this trilogy, which I find so very annoying.<br/><br/>Here we read about FBI agent Jane Hawk. Jane is trying to find out the truth, as to why her husband Nick and many others suddenly commit suicide. She sells her house, leaves her young son wi</span>
  <span id="freeText6327698030875170074" style="display:none">Koontz is one of my favourite authors, but I've not read any of his books for years. Over the years, I have seen the 'series' of books become more and more popular with authors. Having read The Silent Corner, I now have to wait months for the next instalment of the this trilogy, which I find so very annoying.<br /><br />Here we read about FBI agent Jane Hawk. Jane is trying to find out the truth, as to why her husband Nick and many others suddenly commit suicide. She sells her house, leaves her young son with friends, and goes under the radar to find the people responsible.<br /><br />On her route to discovering the truth, Jane ensnares people to help with her information gathering. However, because these are unsavoury characters, Jane terminates their lives mainly to keep both her son and herself safe.<br /><br />Trusting people is not easy, but she crosses paths with an ex army hero and enlists his help. In the meantime, her FBI boss (who is more like a father to Jane) is having doubts that Jane has actually gone rogue and starts to believe that she and her son are actually in danger. A twist in the story there.<br /><br />The ending of the book is a cliff hanger. There are the opening chapters of book 2 to read at the end of the book, but these are merely fishing bait to draw you in to purchasing book 2. Hopefully I won't have to wait too long for books 2 and 3 to be published!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6327698030875170074" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GZC2WZ9ZTT79VcYwDrgDT53HtfE0GUJvK8TIQMInhISHx3q31FQiQAhHwC3AlkYF/jjj4TEzKXp8WAeHP4KTXw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jJGeCkTK/witVtZZxA0I6nVixIALwPlxE7/7tG+7DDMSxlLkD8eQdlhE0EQKI02gFp2SkA7qkmREIzRzkh4b6A==')})
  }

But since its rechristening in the 1970s as a luxury apartment building, the Pendleton has been at peace. For its fortunate residents—among them a successful songwriter and her young son, a disgraced ex-senator, a widowed attorney, and a driven money manager—the Pendleton’s magnificent quarters are a sanctuary, its dark past all but forgotten.\n\nBut now inexplicable shadows caper across walls, security cameras relay impossible images, phantom voices mutter in strange tongues, not-quite-human figures lurk in the basement, elevators plunge into unknown depths. Kett is dragged into the centre of one of the darkest cases of his career — a case that pits him head to head against a horrifying evil.  And a case that might uncover the terrible truth of what happened to his wife.  Terrifying and unputdownable, the first crime novel from million-selling author Alex Smith is officially “a gripping debut” (J. D. Kirk).  Alex Smith wrote his first book when he was six. It wasn’t particularly good, but it did have some supernatural monsters in it. His latest book, Paper Girls, the first DCI Robert Kett thriller, has monsters in it too, although these monsters are very human, and all the more terrifying for it. In between these two books he has published twelve other novels for children and teenagers under his full name, Alexander Gordon Smith—including the number one bestselling series Escape From Furnace, which is loved by millions of readers worldwide and which is soon to become a motion picture. He lives in Norwich with his wife and three young daughters.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"10262020931680344713\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return false;\">...more<\/a>\n\n
